# <a name="encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="34a4a-103">加密链</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="34a4a-103">Encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="34a4a-104">Office 365 利用了许多不同的证书提供程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="34a4a-104">Office 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="34a4a-105">下面介绍了客户在访问 Office 365 时可能遇到的已知 Office 365 根证书的完整列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="34a4a-105">The following describes the complete list of known Office 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="34a4a-106">有关您可能需要在自己的基础结构中安装的证书的信息，请参阅[Plan for 第三方 SSL 证书（适用于 Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates)）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="34a4a-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Office 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="34a4a-107">以下证书信息适用于 Office 365 的所有全球云实例和国家/地区。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="34a4a-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Office 365.</span></span>

>[!NOTE]
><span data-ttu-id="34a4a-108">有关适用于**DOD 和 GCC 高级**客户的证书信息，请参阅[Office 365 加密链-DOD 和 gcc high](encryption-office-365-certificate-chains-itar.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="34a4a-108">For certificate information that applies to **DOD and GCC High** customers, see [Office 365 encryption chains - DOD and GCC High](encryption-office-365-certificate-chains-itar.md).</span></span>
